***некий.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:некий.html>некий</a> (1115)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:некий.html>не́кий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nékij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>a certain, certain
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:некий.html>не́кий</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:гражданин.html>граждани́н</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:распространить.html>распространи́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:слух.html>слух</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Nékij</b> graždanín rasprostraníl slux</i> ― <span class="e-translation">A certain citizen spread a rumor.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:некий.html>не́кая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:женщина.html>же́нщина</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nékaja</b> žénščina</i> ― <span class="e-translation">a certain woman</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>some</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">како́й-то</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kakój-to</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">кое-како́й</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">koje-kakój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:некоторый.html>не́который</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nékotoryj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:известный.html>изве́стный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">izvéstnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:определенный.html>определённый</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">opredeljónnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:некогда.html>некогда</a> (2154)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:некогда.html>не́когда</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nékogda</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>there is no time to (negative of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:когда.html>когда́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kogdá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Мне</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:некогда.html>не́когда</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Mne <b>nékogda</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">I have no time.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>in the old days, in former times, formerly, once
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:некогда.html>не́когда</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:знаменитый.html>знамени́тое</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:учение.html>уче́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nékogda</b> znamenítoje učénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">a once-famous doctrine</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>N.B.— Put the noun or pronoun in the dative case and use the infinitive of a verb.</li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:некого.html>не́кого</a> (3696)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun_2">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:некого.html>не́кого</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nékovo</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>there is no one to (negative genitive of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кто.html>кто</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kto</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Мне</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:некого.html>не́кого</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:винить.html>вини́ть</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Mne <b>nékovo</b> vinítʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I have no one to blame.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Мне</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:некого.html>не́кому</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:писать.html>писа́ть</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Mne nékomu pisátʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I have no one to write to (dative case)</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Put the noun or pronoun in the dative case and use the infinitive of a verb.</li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:некоммерческий.html>некомме́рческий</a> (22654)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:коммерческий.html>комме́рческий</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kommérčeskij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>non-commercial

***некоторый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:некоторый.html>не́который</a> (227)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:некоторый.html>не́который</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nékotoryj</span>) (<i>plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:некоторый.html>не́которые</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>some; certain <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">adjectival</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:некоторый.html>не́которое</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мя</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nékotoroje</b> vrémja</i> ― <span class="e-translation">some time</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:некоторый.html>не́которой</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:степень.html>сте́пени</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">do <b>nékotoroj</b> stépeni</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to <b>some</b> extent; to a <b>certain</b> extent</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:некоторый.html>не́котором</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>ро́де</a></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">formal usage</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v <b>nékotorom</b> róde</i> ― <span class="e-translation">kind of, sort of; in <b>some</b> way</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">plural only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> some, some people; certain people <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">pronominal</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:некоторый.html>не́которые</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:они.html>них</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nékotoryje</b> iz nix</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>some</b> of them</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:некоторый.html>не́которые</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:думать.html>ду́мают</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:черепаха.html>черепа́хи</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:жить.html>живу́т</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:долго.html>до́лго</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Nékotoryje</b> dúmajut, što čerepáxi živút dólgo.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>Some</b> think tortoises live a long time.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:некстати.html>некста́ти</a> (11826)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кстати.html>кста́ти</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kstáti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:некстати.html>некста́ти</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nekstáti</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>inopportunely, malapropos, at the wrong moment
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прийти.html>прийти́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:некстати.html>некста́ти</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">prijtí <b>nekstáti</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to be unwelcome</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>irrelevantly, out of place, ineptly
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сказать.html>сказа́ть</a> что́-либо <b><a href = vnd.unilang:некстати.html>некста́ти</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">skazátʹ štó-libo <b>nekstáti</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">say something out of place (not to the point)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кстати.html>кста́ти</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:некстати.html>некста́ти</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kstáti i <b>nekstáti</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">in season and out of season</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***некто.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:некто.html>некто</a> (5625)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:некто.html>не́кто</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nékto</span>) (<i>indeclinable, invariable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">indefinite pronoun</span>, somebody, someone
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:некто.html>не́кто</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:узнать.html>узна́ет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:об.html>об</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́том</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Nékto</b> uznájet ob étom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Someone will find out about this.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>a certain
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:некто.html>не́кто</a></b> па́влов</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Nékto</b> Pávlov</i> ― <span class="e-translation">A certain Mr. Pavlov; one Mr. Pavlov.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Only used in nominative and accusative cases, with no oblique declensions.</li>
<li>The term is indeclinable. The inflected forms <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:некого.html>не́кого</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nékovo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:некого.html>не́кому</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nékomu</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:некого.html>не́кем</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nékem</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> are related but have a different meaning.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">кто́-то</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">któ-to</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">кто́-либо</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">któ-libo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неладный.html>нела́дный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">neládnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неладный.html>нела́дно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">neládno</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>amiss <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">wrong</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>С</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ним</a> что́-то <b><a href = vnd.unilang:неладный.html>нела́дно</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">S nim štó-to <b>neládno</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">There is something <b>amiss</b> with him.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нелегкий.html>нелёгкий</a> (6516)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нелегкий.html>нелёгкий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">neljóxkij</span>)
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нелепый.html>неле́пый</a> (3428)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нелепый.html>неле́пый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nelépyj</span>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нельзя.html>нельзя́</a> (277)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">нельзѣ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nelĭzě</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">нельзѧ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nelĭzę</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">нельза</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nelĭza</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*ne</i> / <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*ně</i> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*lьga</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">possibility</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (possibly influenced by its dative <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*lьdzě</i>), likely related to <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*lьgъkъ</i> (whence <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">лёгкий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ljóxkij</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">light, easy</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>).
</p><p>Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">не́льга</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nélʹha</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">нільга́</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nilʹhá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk"><a href = vnd.unilang:нельзя.html>нельзя́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nelʹzjá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belarusian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Belarusian language">Belarusian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be">няльга́</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">njalʹhá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be">нільга́</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nilʹhá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be">не́льга</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">njélʹha</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">льзѣ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lĭzě</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">possible, possibly</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovak_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovak language">Slovak</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sk">nelza</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="sk">nelzä</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="sk">neľzä</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Old Polish language">Old Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="zlw-opl">nielza</i>, also modern <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovene_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovene language">Slovene</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sl">lahko</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">may, be allowed</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Predicative">Predicative</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нельзя.html>нельзя́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nelʹzjá</span>) <i>(impersonal, invariable)</i>
</p>
<ol><li>it is impossible <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">perfective aspect</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, one cannot, you can't
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:нельзя.html>нельзя́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> + <i>perfective infinitive</i></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nelʹzjá</b> jemú + <i>perfective infinitive</i></i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>it is impossible</b> for him to (perfective infinitive)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>it is prohibited <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">imperfective aspect</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, it is forbidden, it is not allowed, one must not
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:здесь.html>здесь</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:нельзя.html>нельзя́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:курить.html>кури́ть</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">zdesʹ <b>nelʹzjá</b> kurítʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>it is not allowed</b> to smoke here</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>one cannot
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:нельзя.html>нельзя́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:заметить.html>заме́тить</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:влюбиться.html>влюби́лся</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>неё</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nelʹzjá</b> ne zamétitʹ, što on vljubílsja v nejó</i> ― <span class="e-translation">One cannot fail to notice that he has fallen in love with her</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:нельзя.html>нельзя́</a></b> is the negative of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:можно.html>мо́жно</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">móžno</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Instead of saying <b><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:можно.html>мо́жно</a></b>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:нельзя.html>нельзя́</a></b> should be always used.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
